 mamata ne samiti kaa gathan pichley saal may main rajya kii satta sambhaalane ke baad kiya tha

 What is the importance of Akshay III: - In Hindu scriptures, the day of Akshay III is considered to be the most auspicious
 - baishakh maheene ke shukla paksh kii tritiy tithi ko manaai jane vaali akshay tritiy behad laabhakaari he
 - It is believed that Satyuga and Treta Yuga started from this date
 - 9 may ko akshay tritiy kaa paavan muhoort pad rahaa he
 - Akshay means never destroyed
 - is din sona khareednaa, sone kaa upyog karnaa bahutfaldaayihota he
 According to mythological beliefs, we get manifold results of the auspicious work done on this day
 akshay tritiy par grahon kaa shubh sanyog :- is din grahon kaa vishesh sanyog banataa he
 - Sun and Moon are in their highest zodiac sign
 - saal main sirf ek din ye sanyog banataa he
 - Sun is in Aries and Moon is in Taurus
 - shastron main surya ko hamaara praan or chandramaa ko hamaara man mana gaya he
 - Due to the relationship between Sun and Moon, this date becomes very important
 - isliye is din jo bhi kaam kiya jaae uskaa fal doguna or kabhi na khatm hone vaala hoga
 Do this auspicious work on this day: - Akshaya Tritiya can be done related to wedding, home-entry, purchase of clothes and jewelry or purchase of house, land, car
 - is din nayaa kapadaa, jevar pahananaa or nai sanstha or kaam kaa udghaatan shubh mana jaataa he
 - It is a mythological belief that on this day, the tarpan and pinddan or any kind of donation made to the ancestral side gives akshaya
 - is din kiya gaya ganga snaan or pujan sabhi paapon ko nasht karata he
 Every person wishes for prosperity
 isi vajah se is din sona kharidne se vah akshay matlab kabhi na khatm hone vaala hoga
 - The chanting, penance, havan, puja, donation performed on Akshaya Tritiya increases manifold
 - is din hamen sadgunon ke liye prarthana kerani chahie or jane anjaane main kiye gaye paapon kii kshamaa yachana kerani chahie
